[30;1m105 | [0m[35mWhy is this important?[0m
[30;1m106 | [0m[35m======================[0m
[30;1m107 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m108 | [0m[35mThe usage of a FST might not be obvious at first sight so let's consider a[0m
[30;1m109 | [0m[35mseries of problems to illustrate it. Let's say that you want to write a program that will:[0m
